<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:puberaal.html>puberaal</a> (48638)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably borrowed, cf. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">puberal</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:puberale.html>puberale</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puber.html>puber</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aal</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puber.html>puber</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-teit</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">puberté</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pubertas</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the age of maturity, manhood</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pubes</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:puber.html>puber</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grown up, of mature age, adult; of plants, downy, pubescent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puffen.html>puffen</a></strong>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:puffen.html>puffen</a></i>, sharing an imitative <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> base with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">pyffan</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:puffen.html>puffen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">puff</i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puffen.html>puffen</a></strong>

<ol><li>to puff, blow out (hot air, such as the chugging of a steam engine)</li></ol>

***pug.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a> (50897)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Pug_portrait.jpg/220px-Pug_portrait.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Pug_portrait.jpg/330px-Pug_portrait.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Pug_portrait.jpg/440px-Pug_portrait.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3888" data-file-height="2592" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>portrait of a <a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></div></div></div>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pugs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A small dog of an ancient breed originating in China, having a snub nose, wrinkled face, squarish body, short smooth hair, and curled tail. <span class="defdate">[from the 18th c]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">Chinese <a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">Dutch bulldog</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">Dutch <a href = vnd.unilang:mastiff.html>mastiff</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">mini <a href = vnd.unilang:mastiff.html>mastiff</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mops.html>mops</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:carlin.html>carlin</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">pugdog</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A bargeman. <span class="defdate">[from the 16th c]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chaff; the refuse of grain
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Holland to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>Any geometrid moth of the genus <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Eupithecia" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Eupithecia"><i>Eupithecia</i></a></span>.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a> nose</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">pug-nosed</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">pug-ugly</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Corruption of <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:puck.html>puck</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">pūca</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:goblin.html>goblin</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:demon.html>demon</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.  Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">púki</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:demon.html>demon</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">pwca</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hobgoblin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pugs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An <a href = vnd.unilang:elf.html>elf</a> or hobgoblin.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>Ben</a> Jonson to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>An upper servant in a great house. <span class="defdate">[from the 19th c]</span></li>
<li>A harlot; a prostitute. <span class="defdate">[circa 1600]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Cotgrave to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">mythological creature</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:puck.html>puck</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:goblin.html>goblin</a>, fairy</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Abbreviation of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pugilist</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pugil</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pugs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One who <a href = vnd.unilang:fights.html>fights</a> with fists; a boxer.
<ul><li><b>1988</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ken.html>Ken</a> Blady, <i>The Jewish <a href = vnd.unilang:boxers.html>Boxers</a> Hall of Fame</i> (page 226)
<dl><dd>He never trained for his characters either: with his slurred speech and disfigured mug he usually portrayed a punch-drunk ex-<b><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></b> or comic tough guy, roles in which he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a natural.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">pucken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to thump, beat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pugs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any compressed clay-like material mixed and worked into a soft, plastic condition for making <a href = vnd.unilang:bricks.html>bricks</a>, pottery or for paving. (Also <i><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a> soil</i>)</li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a> mill.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">pugs</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">pugging</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">pugged</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To mix and stir when <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a>.
<dl><dd><i>to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a> for <a href = vnd.unilang:bricks.html>bricks</a> or pottery</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To fill or <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a> with <a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a> by tamping; to fill in or spread with mortar, as a floor or partition, for the purpose of deadening sound.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology 5</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi">Hindi</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="hi">पग</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pag</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">step, foot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">पद्य</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">padya</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">foot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Greek language">Greek</a></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">πόδι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pódi</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">foot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pug.html>pug</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">pugs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The pawprint or footprint of an animal</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">pugmark</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology 6</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably related to <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:puck.html>puck</a></span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puin.html>puin</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wreckage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">heap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***pulsen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pulsen.html>pulsen</a> (44806)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> derived from the name of a moving company Abraham <a href = vnd.unilang:puls.html>Puls</a> amp; Sons, employed by the Nazi-led Dutch police to pillage and empty the homes of the 140,000 Jews of the Netherlands during the Holocaust.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pulsen.html>pulsen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to violently dispossess, to loot, to destroy property and environment, of Jews in particular.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pulsen.html>pulsen</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">overgankelijk</span> <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:bouwkunde.html>bouwkunde</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> grondboormethode: <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:buis.html>buis</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> onderen open <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:diepte.html>diepte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drukken.html>drukken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grond.html>grond</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paal.html>paal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:scheppen.html>scheppen</a></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:stelen.html>stelen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:huizen.html>huizen</a> leeghalen (<a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:joden.html>Joden</a>) <sup id="cite_ref-qpulsen_3-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-qpulsen-3"> | 3 | </a></sup></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>Either borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:punker.html>punker</a></i> or natively formed from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">punk</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:punt.html>punt</a> (1009)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">punctum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:punt.html>punt</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:punten.html>punten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puntje.html>puntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">point</span>
<ol><li>A position, place, or spot</li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a> in time</li>
<li>A central idea, argument, or opinion of a discussion or presentation</li>
<li>A tally of worth or score (such as in a game)</li>
<li>A mark, note, or grade (as in for a class)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geometry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> geometric point
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>Door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:punten.html>punten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:precies.html>precies</a> één <a href = vnd.unilang:rechte.html>rechte</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Through two points one can draw exactly one straight line.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">point</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">punctus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:punt.html>punt</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:punten.html>punten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:puntje.html>puntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The terminal point of something
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:punt.html>punt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naald.html>naald</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:mes.html>mes</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the point of a needle or knife</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> zuidpunt <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eiland.html>eiland</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the southern point of the island</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>dot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> ypsilon, <a href = vnd.unilang:zonder.html>zonder</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:puntjes.html>puntjes</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">A wye, without dots on it.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>full <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a>, period
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>Aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:einde.html>einde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zin.html>zin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoort.html>hoort</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:punt.html>punt</a></b> of <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ander.html>ander</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leesteken.html>leesteken</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">At the end of a sentence there <a href = vnd.unilang:belongs.html>belongs</a> a full <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a> or another punctuation sign.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:punt.html>Punt</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gedaan.html>gedaan</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Full <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a>, finished. / That’s it, period.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A pointy slice of a cake, pie or <a href = vnd.unilang:pizza.html>pizza</a>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">taartpunt</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***purper.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:purper.html>purper</a> (48633)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:purper.html>purper</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">purpura</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πορφύρα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porphúra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:purper.html>purper</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:purper.html>purpers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>purple, especially a reddish hue of purple <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">colour</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with definite article</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The purple, imperial or royal power, in particular in relation to the Roman Empire
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:legeraanvoerder.html>legeraanvoerder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:liet.html>liet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoon.html>zoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:purper.html>purper</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:aannemen.html>aannemen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The military commander let his son adopt the <b>purple</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">purperen</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">purperreiger</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">purperslak</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:purper.html>purper</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> purple
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paars.html>paars</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pigmene</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Pygmies</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Pygmaeī</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πυγμαῖος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pugmaîos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pygmee.html>pygmee</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pygmee.html>pygmeeën</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A pygmy <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">member of an African tribe of short people</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li>A pygmy animal, a dwarf animal.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwerg.html>dwerg</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncommon</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An insignificant person, a pygmy.</li></ol>
<hr />

</p>

***pyjama.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pyjama.html>pyjama</a> (7042)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pajamas</i>, from <i>pai jamahs</i> (“loose trousers tied at the waist, worn by Muslims in India”), adopted by colonials, especially for nightwear, probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi">Hindi</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="hi">पैजामा</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">paijāmā</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pajama</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">پایجامه</i> | .
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>pyjamas, a matching set of light material trousers and <a href = vnd.unilang:vest.html>vest</a> for wearing to <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a> and sleeping in</li></ol>
